2026-05-19T21:20:15.3462850Z [36;1mecho "[3/10] Binary Architecture Check"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3462990Z [36;1mecho "---------------------------------"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3463120Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3463210Z [36;1mfor BIN in "$VST3_BIN" "$CLAP_BIN"; do[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3463490Z [36;1m  echo "Checking $(basename $(dirname $(dirname $BIN)))/$(basename $BIN)..."[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3463680Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3463760Z [36;1m  # Must be Mach-O universal[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3463980Z [36;1m  file "$BIN" | grep -q "Mach-O universal binary" || error "Not a Mach-O universal binary: $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3464190Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3464280Z [36;1m  # Must contain both architectures[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3464420Z [36;1m  LIPO_OUT=$(lipo -info "$BIN" 2>&1)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3464540Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3464700Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT" | grep -q "x86_64" || error "Missing x86_64 in $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3464930Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT" | grep -q "arm64" || error "Missing arm64 in $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3465090Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3465210Z [36;1m  # Binary size check (should be > 1MB for a real plugin)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3465430Z [36;1m  SIZE=$(stat -f%z "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || stat -c%s "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3465620Z [36;1m  if [ "$SIZE" -lt 1048576 ]; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3465780Z [36;1m    error "Binary suspiciously small ($SIZE bytes): $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466000Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466090Z [36;1m  echo "Binary size: $SIZE bytes"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466210Z [36;1mdone[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466280Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466370Z [36;1mecho "Binary architecture: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466480Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466580Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466720Z [36;1m# 4. CODE SIGNATURE INTEGRITY[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466860Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3466990Z [36;1mecho ""[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467080Z [36;1mecho "[4/10] Code Signature Check"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467280Z [36;1mecho "----------------------------"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467400Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467480Z [36;1mfor BUNDLE in "$VST3" "$CLAP"; do[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467620Z [36;1m  echo "Checking $(basename $BUNDLE)..."[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467740Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3467880Z [36;1m  # Strict signature verification (no --deep here, check bundle itself)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3468160Z [36;1m  codesign -vvv "$BUNDLE" || error "Signature verification failed for $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3468370Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3468450Z [36;1m  # Verify signature is ad-hoc[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3468750Z [36;1m  CS_INFO=$(codesign -dvv "$BUNDLE" 2>&1)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3468910Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3469120Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "Signature=adhoc" || error "Not ad-hoc signed: $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3469430Z [36;1m    # Allow either adhoc,runtime or just adhoc (macOS 15+ can't embed entitlements ad-hoc)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3469680Z [36;1m    if echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "adhoc,runtime"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3469850Z [36;1m      echo "  Hardened runtime: enabled"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3470110Z [36;1m    else[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3470320Z [36;1m      echo "  Hardened runtime: disabled (expected — ad-hoc on macOS 15+ can't embed entitlements)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3470550Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3470630Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3470730Z [36;1m  # Verify CodeDirectory exists and is sealed[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3470980Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "Sealed Resources" || error "Sealed Resources missing: $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3471380Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3471560Z [36;1m  # Check that no files are modified after signing[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3471760Z [36;1m  if codesign -vvv "$BUNDLE" 2>&1 | grep -qi "modified"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3471970Z [36;1m    error "Files modified after signing in $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472130Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472210Z [36;1mdone[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472290Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472370Z [36;1mecho "Code signature: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472480Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472580Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3472790Z [36;1m# 5. ENTITLEMENTS (skip if no hardened runtime — ad-hoc on macOS 15+ can't embed)[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473190Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473320Z [36;1mecho ""[0m

2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473550Z [36;1mecho "-------------------------"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473670Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473750Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements() {[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473860Z [36;1m  local BIN="$1"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3473960Z [36;1m  local NAME="$2"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3474090Z [36;1m  local CS_INFO=$(codesign -dvv "$BIN" 2>&1 || echo "")[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3474270Z [36;1m  if echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "runtime"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3474440Z [36;1m    # Hardened runtime is enabled — check entitlements[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3474670Z [36;1m    local ENTITLEMENTS=$(codesign -d --entitlements - "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || echo "")[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3474890Z [36;1m    if [ -z "$ENTITLEMENTS" ]; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3475060Z [36;1m      error "No entitlements found in $NAME (has hardened runtime)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3475230Z [36;1m    else[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3475450Z [36;1m      echo "$ENTITLEMENTS" | grep -q "com.apple.security.cs.disable-library-validation" || \[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3475750Z [36;1m        error "Missing disable-library-validation entitlement in $NAME"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3475940Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476020Z [36;1m  else[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476180Z [36;1m    echo "SKIP: $NAME has no hardened runtime — entitlements not applicable"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476370Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476460Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476540Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476640Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements "$VST3_BIN" "VST3"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476790Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements "$CLAP_BIN" "CLAP"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3476920Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3477020Z [36;1mecho "Entitlements: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3477130Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:20:15.3477230Z [36;1m# ============================================================[0m
